***gallisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gallisch.html>gallisch</a> (130945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">חלש</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khallish</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nauseous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">חַלָשׁ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chalash</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>Said</a> to be used in theatre circles originally. Probably an association with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geil.html>geil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gallig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">choleric</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> made, whence the senses <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">angry</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hot</i>, an instance of folk etymology.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gallisch.html>gallisch</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>nauseous</li>
<li>angry, irritated</li>
<li>hot, sensuous, <a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gallisch.html>gallisch</a></b>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> word <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gallisch.html>gallisch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gamba.html>gamba</a> (106650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:viola.html>viola</a> da <a href = vnd.unilang:gamba.html>gamba</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamba.html>gamba</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamba.html>gamba</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamba.html>gamba</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamba.html>gambaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">*<a href = vnd.unilang:gammel.html>gammel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">*gamal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*gamal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gamalaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gamel</i>.
</p>

***gander.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>gander</a> (75916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Most likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>gander</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>gander</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ndl">ganner</i>. Both are possibly formed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">goose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in an analogous way as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kater.html>kater</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(female) cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doffer.html>doffer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male <a href = vnd.unilang:dove.html>dove</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duif.html>duif</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(female) <a href = vnd.unilang:dove.html>dove</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>gander</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>ganders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>gandertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>gander</a></a>, male goose</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">male goose</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ganzerik</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gent.html>gent</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">mannetjesgans</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ganc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gank</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gangaz</i>.

***ganglion.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ganglion.html>ganglion</a> (93353)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γαγγλίον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ganglíon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">encysted tumour on a tendon, anything gathered into a ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganglion.html>ganglion</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ganglions</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganglia.html>ganglia</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neuroanatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<ol><li>An encapsulated collection of nerve-cell <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a>, located outside the brain and spinal cord.</li>
<li>Any of certain masses of gray matter in the brain, as the basal <a href = vnd.unilang:ganglia.html>ganglia</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> August 3,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.economist.com/news/science-and-technology/21582495-computers-will-help-people-understand-brains-better-and-understanding-brains">The machine of a new soul</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Economist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Economist">The Economist</a></cite>, volume 408, number 8847:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The yawning gap in neuroscientists’ understanding of their topic <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the intermediate scale of the brain’s anatomy. Science <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a passable knowledge of how individual nerve cells, known as neurons, work. It also knows which visible lobes and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganglia.html>ganglia</a></b> of the brain do what. But how the neurons are organised in these lobes and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganglia.html>ganglia</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> obscure.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A centre of intellectual or industrial force, activity, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cystic tumour on a tendon sheath or joint capsule; a <a href = vnd.unilang:ganglion.html>ganglion</a> cyst.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganglion.html>ganglion</a></b> ; <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span> zenuwknoop</li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:holte.html>holte</a> in of <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> gewrichtskapsel of peesschede <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevuld.html>gevuld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geelachtige.html>geelachtige</a> glijstof</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gangreen.html>gangreen</a> (35150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gangraena</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γάγγραινα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gángraina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gangreen.html>gangreen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>gangrene
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">koudvuur</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***gans.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a> (7052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></i> (alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gōs</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gās</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰans-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>Gans</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Goos</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>Gans</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">goes</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">goose</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">gås</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Anser_indicus2.jpg/250px-Anser_indicus2.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="179" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Anser_indicus2.jpg/375px-Anser_indicus2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Anser_indicus2.jpg/500px-Anser_indicus2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="536" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:indische.html>Indische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></i><br />Bar-headed goose (<i>literally:</i> Indian goose)</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganzen.html>ganzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gansje.html>gansje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A goose, a waterfowl of the family Anatidae, especially of the subfamily Anserinae excepting the genera <i>Cygnus</i> and <i>Coscoroba</i>; in non-scientific usage the term may be applied to larger waterfowl of the Anatidae who do not belong to the Anserinae.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gansch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gands</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gants.html>gants</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gantaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all, whole, entire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***gant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gant.html>gant</a> (14359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">guant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*want</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">want</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wantus</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wantuz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">guanto</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">guante</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca">guant</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:gant.html>gant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:gants.html>gants</a></b>)
</p>

***ganz.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a> (31909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whole, sound, healthy, complete, fullstanding</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gantaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whole, sound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰen-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flourish, be full, swell, abound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></i> (borrowed from Old High German).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>entire; whole; complete
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">gesamt</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">komplett</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> hat ein <b>ganzes</b> Hähnchen gegessen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> a <b>whole</b> chicken.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Der_Spiegel" class="extiw" title="w:Der Spiegel"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>Der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spiegel.html>Spiegel</a></a></i>, issue <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.spiegel.de/spiegel/print/index-2010-33.html">33/2010</a>, page 83:
<dl><dd>Seit Ende <a href = vnd.unilang:juli.html>Juli</a> hat <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Monsunregen <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Flüsse in weiten <a href = vnd.unilang:teil.html>Teilen</a> Pakistans über <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Ufer treten <a href = vnd.unilang:lassen.html>lassen</a> und <b>ganze</b> Provinzen in Seen verwandelt
<dl><dd>Since end of July the monsoon rain <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> made the rivers overflow their <a href = vnd.unilang:banks.html>banks</a> in large parts of Pakistan and <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> whole provinces into lakes.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> all <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with definite article or determiner</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">all</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Ich hab <a href = vnd.unilang:meine.html>meine</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganzen.html>ganzen</a></b> Freunde eingeladen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve invited <b>all</b> my friends.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whole; intact
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:heil.html>heil</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">intakt</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">unversehrt</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Ist <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Tasse <a href = vnd.unilang:noch.html>noch</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> the cup still <b>whole</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in certain combinations</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> true; real
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">wahr</span></span></dd>
<dd><i>ein <b>ganzer</b> Kerl</i> — “a <b>true</b> man” <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">implying masculinity, but also uprightness</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> integer (of a number)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>quite, rather
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">ziemlich</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>very
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sehr.html>sehr</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1918</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/de:Elisabeth_von_Heyking" class="extiw" title="w:de:Elisabeth von Heyking">Elisabeth von Heyking</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/de:Aus_dem_Lande_der_Ostseeritter" class="extiw" title="s:de:Aus dem Lande der Ostseeritter">Aus dem <a href = vnd.unilang:lande.html>Lande</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Ostseeritter</a></i>, in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zwei.html>Zwei</a> Erzählungen</i>, Phillipp Reclam jun., page 73:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> Herrenhaus in Burkahnen war ein <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></b> altes Gebäude, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>
<dl><dd>The manor house in Burkahnen <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a very old building, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>wholly, entirely, all
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">komplett</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">völlig</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1903</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fanny_zu_Reventlow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fanny zu Reventlow"><a href = vnd.unilang:fanny.html>Fanny</a> zu Reventlow</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/de:Ellen_Olestjerne" class="extiw" title="s:de:Ellen Olestjerne"><a href = vnd.unilang:ellen.html>Ellen</a> Olestjerne</a></i>, in <i>Franziska Gräfin zu Reventlow: Gesammelte <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>Werke</a></i>, Albert <a href = vnd.unilang:langen.html>Langen</a>, page 580:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> Kirche war <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Sonne leuchtete <a href = vnd.unilang:durch.html>durch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Bogenfenster, und droben spielte jemand auf <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:orgel.html>Orgel</a>.
<dl><dd>The church <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> entirely empty, the sun shone through the arched <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a> and up there someone played the organ.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***gar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a> (28216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:gare.html>gare</a></i> (inflected <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">garw-</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">garo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garwaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaar.html>gaar</a></i>, archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">keen, lively, eager</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related with <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gerben</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>cooked, done <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of food such as meat or vegetables: ready for consumption</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> at all; <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">überhaupt</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sie.html>Sie</a> hat <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></b> kein <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>Geld</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no money <b>at all</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> ist <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kommen.html>gekommen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> show up. / He didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> show up <b>at all</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Der_Spiegel" class="extiw" title="w:Der Spiegel"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>Der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spiegel.html>Spiegel</a></a></i>, issue <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.spiegel.de/spiegel/print/index-2010-25.html">25/2010</a>, page 80:
<dl><dd>Ein Verbot sollte es <a href = vnd.unilang:nach.html>nach</a> Ansicht vieler Ökonomen auch für <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> sogenannten Leerverkäufe geben. <a href = vnd.unilang:banken.html>Banken</a> verkaufen dabei Aktien <a href = vnd.unilang:oder.html>oder</a> Währungen, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sie.html>sie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noch.html>noch</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nicht.html>nicht</a> besitzen <a href = vnd.unilang:oder.html>oder</a> allenfalls geliehen <a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a>.
<dl><dd>In the opinion of many economists, there should also exist a prohibition for the so-called short sales. In these, <a href = vnd.unilang:banks.html>banks</a> sell shares or currencies that they do not own at all yet or have borrowed at <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly formal or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a>; <span class="use-with-mention">expressing a climax</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">sogar</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">selbst</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">geradezu</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Ist <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> ein Dieb? Ein Räuber? <a href = vnd.unilang:oder.html>Oder</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></b> ein Mörder?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> he a thief? <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly formal or literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zu</i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> all
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">all, <i>usually <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a></i> allzu</span></span></dd>

***garen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garen</a> (17507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*garn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*garn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>yarn, thread</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaar.html>gaar</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make/become ready (cooked)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Syncopic form of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gaderen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gāderen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gadaron</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*gadurōn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:garen.html>garen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collect, to gather</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:garr.html>garr</a> (70031)</h1><br></body> 
***garret.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:garret.html>garret</a> (14961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">garett</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">garite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">garite</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">guerite</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">watchtower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">garir</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">guarir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to defend, protect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">garrison</i>), ultimately of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> origin (see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:garage.html>garage</a></i>). Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">guerite</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:garret.html>garret</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">garrets</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An attic or semi-finished room just beneath the roof of a house.
<ul><li><b>1660</b>, Samuel Pepys Diary<i>, January 1.</i>
<dl><dd>This morning (<a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> living lately in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:garret.html>garret</a></b>,) I <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a>, put on my suit with great skirts, having not lately worn any other <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> but them.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1866</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoevsky" class="extiw" title="w:Fyodor Dostoevsky">Fyodor Dostoyevsky</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> by <a href = vnd.unilang:constance.html>Constance</a> Garnett),  <cite>Crime and Punishment</cite> | <sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Crime_and_Punishment/Part_I/Chapter_I">[1]</a></sup>, Part I, Chapter I:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">On an exceptionally hot evening early in July a young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> out of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:garret.html>garret</a></b> in which he lodged in S. Place and walked slowly, as though in hesitation, towards K. bridge.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1895</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_MacDonald" class="extiw" title="w:George MacDonald">George MacDonald</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:lilith.html>Lilith</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in the main <b><a href = vnd.unilang:garret.html>garret</a></b>, with huge beams and <a href = vnd.unilang:rafters.html>rafters</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> my head, great spaces around <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> here and there in sight, and long vistas whose gloom <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> thinned by a few lurking cobwebbed <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a> and small dusky skylights.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> February 22,  <a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> J. Wakin,  “Free Trove of Music <a href = vnd.unilang:scores.html>Scores</a> on Web <a href = vnd.unilang:hits.html>Hits</a> Sensitive Copyright Note”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/22/arts/music/22music-imslp.html">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">While a boon to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:garret.html>garret</a></b>-living, financially struggling young musicians, the library <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> caught the attention of music publishers.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">gartier</i>, from lang="fro">jaret</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" mention" lang="cel-pro">*garros</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">calf, <a href = href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cornish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Cornish language">Cornish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kw"><a href = vnd.unilang:gar.html>gar</a></i>, <span ***gaspedaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaspedaal.html>gaspedaal</a> (16123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gas</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pedaal.html>pedaal</a></i>, perhaps a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gaspedal</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gas pedal</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***gastritis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gastritis.html>gastritis</a> (93335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γαστήρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gastḗr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-itis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inflammation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gastritis.html>gastritis</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gastritides</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Inflammation of the lining of the stomach, characterised by nausea, loss of appetite, and upper abdominal discomfort or pain.</li></ol>
